commit 0250c7489066c36120ca01432cac0aaee461d57e
Author: Trevor Bača <trevorbaca@gmail.com>
Date:   Thu Apr 2 22:33:10 2015 -0400

    Added DurationBeatMaker to rhythmmakertools. NEW.
    
    Models one way of decomposing meters into beats.
    
    Maker decomposes meters into beats of approximately equal duration.
    Affordances allow the duration of beats in simple and compound meters to be
    set separately. Beats returned as output from this maker can subsequently
    be passed to a beat group maker to assemble conductors' groupings.
    
    Example 1. Makes quarter-note-durated beats for all meters.
    
        >>> maker = rhythmmakertools.DurationBeatMaker(
        ...     compound_beat_duration=Duration(1, 4),
        ...     simple_beat_duration=Duration(1, 4),
        ...     )
    
        Quarter-note-durated beats for simple meters:
    
        >>> maker([metertools.Meter((3, 4))])
        [[Duration(1, 4), Duration(1, 4), Duration(1, 4)]]
        >>> maker([metertools.Meter((3, 2))])
        [[Duration(1, 4), Duration(1, 4), Duration(1, 4), Duration(1, 4), Duration(1, 4), Duration(1, 4)]]
    
        Quarter-note-durated beats for compound meters:
    
        >>> maker([metertools.Meter((6, 8))])
        [[Duration(1, 4), Duration(1, 4), Duration(1, 4)]]
        >>> maker([metertools.Meter((6, 4))])
        [[Duration(1, 4), Duration(1, 4), Duration(1, 4), Duration(1, 4), Duration(1, 4), Duration(1, 4)]]
    
    Example 2. Makes dotted-quarter-note-durated beats for all meters.
    
        >>> maker = rhythmmakertools.DurationBeatMaker(
        ...     compound_beat_duration=Duration(3, 8),
        ...     simple_beat_duration=Duration(3, 8),
        ...     )
    
        Dotted-quarter-note-durated beats for simple meters:
    
        >>> maker([metertools.Meter((3, 4))])
        [[Duration(3, 8), Duration(3, 8)]]
        >>> maker([metertools.Meter((3, 2))])
        [[Duration(3, 8), Duration(3, 8), Duration(3, 8), Duration(3, 8)]]
        Dotted-quarter-note-durated beats for compound meters:
    
        >>> maker([metertools.Meter((6, 8))])
        [[Duration(3, 8), Duration(3, 8)]]
        >>> maker([metertools.Meter((6, 4))])
        [[Duration(3, 8), Duration(3, 8), Duration(3, 8), Duration(3, 8)]]
    
    Example 3. Makes quarter-note-durated-beats for simple meters and
    dotted-quarter-note-durated beats for compound meters.
    
        >>> maker = rhythmmakertools.DurationBeatMaker(
        ...     compound_beat_duration=Duration(3, 8),
        ...     simple_beat_duration=Duration(1, 4),
        ...     )
    
        Quarter-note-durated beats for simple meters:
    
        >>> maker([metertools.Meter((3, 4))])
        [[Duration(1, 4), Duration(1, 4), Duration(1, 4)]]
        >>> maker([metertools.Meter((3, 2))])
        [[Duration(1, 4), Duration(1, 4), Duration(1, 4), Duration(1, 4), Duration(1, 4), Duration(1, 4)]]
        Dotted-quarter-note-durated beats for compound meters:
    
        >>> maker([metertools.Meter((6, 8))])
        [[Duration(3, 8), Duration(3, 8)]]
        >>> maker([metertools.Meter((6, 4))])
        [[Duration(3, 8), Duration(3, 8), Duration(3, 8), Duration(3, 8)]]
    
    NEW: should be included in the 2.16 release notes.
    
    Note that this deprecates Meter.get_beats().

    Implemented BeatGrouper.fuse_assignable_total_duration property.
    
    When true groups of beats that sum to assignable durations will
    be output as assignable durations.
    
    When false groups of beats that sum to assignable durations will be treated
    just like groups of beats that do not sum to assignable durations.

        maker = rhythmmakertools.AccelerandoRhythmMaker(
            start_duration=Duration(1, 8),
            stop_duration=Duration(1, 16),

            music,

        \score {
            \new Score <<
                \new TimeSignatureContext {
                    {
                        \time 5/8
                        s1 * 5/8
                    }
                    {
                        \time 3/8
                        s1 * 3/8
                    }
                }
                \new RhythmicStaff {
                    {
                        \time 5/8
                        c'8 * 31/32 [
                        c'8 * 119/128
                        c'8 * 13/16
                        c'8 * 11/16
                        c'8 * 75/128
                        c'8 * 67/128
                        c'8 * 63/128 ]
                    }
                    {
                        \time 3/8
                        c'8 * 63/64 [
                        c'8 * 55/64
                        c'8 * 41/64

                    }
                }
            >>
        }

commit 39760e8a1477a44d9b7e907cacc8a2cb128e740e
Author: Trevor Bača <trevorbaca@gmail.com>
Date:   Sun Apr 5 17:45:27 2015 -0400

    Added Duration.to_score_markup(). NEW.
    
    Example:
    
        >>> markup = Duration(5, 16).to_score_markup()
        >>> f(markup)
        \markup {
            \score
                {
                    \new Score \with {
                        proportionalNotationDuration = ##f
                    } <<
                        \new RhythmicStaff \with {
                            \remove Time_signature_engraver
                            \remove Staff_symbol_engraver
                            \override Stem #'direction = #up
                            \override Stem #'length = #4
                            \override TupletBracket #'bracket-visibility = ##t
                            \override TupletBracket #'direction = #up
                            \override TupletBracket #'padding = #1.25
                            \override TupletBracket #'shorten-pair = #'(-1 . -1.5)
                            \override TupletNumber #'text = #tuplet-number::calc-fraction-text
                            fontSize = #-2
                            tupletFullLength = ##t
                        } {
                            c'4 ~
                            c'16
                        }
                    >>
                    \layout {
                        indent = #0
                        ragged-right = ##t
                    }
                }
            }
    
    The markup is complicated by perfectly configured to work as an override
    for TupletNumber.text or as either the LHS or RHS of a MetricModulation.
    
    See the Duration API entry for notated examples.
    
    This commit removes an earlier version of this code from MetricModulation.
    
    Note that there is also a private statich Duration._to_score_markup() method
    available to developers of other Abjad classes.
    
    NEW: should be included with notation examples in the 2.16 release notes.

commit adae3fee16d5e9ce0f91a09058d640cf035addb3
Author: Josiah Wolf Oberholtzer <josiah.oberholtzer@gmail.com>
Date:   Sun Apr 5 15:26:14 2015 -0700

    Added configuration methods to PitchOperation.
    
    Each method configures and returns a new pitch operation instance with a new
    operator appended to the list of operators. This behavior mirrors that of
    Selector and Postscript:
    
        PitchOperation.invert() -> Inversion
        PitchOperation.multiply() -> Multiplication
        PitchOperation.retrograde() -> Retrogression()
        PitchOperation.rotate() -> Rotation()
        PitchOperation.transpose() -> Transposition()

commit 574bed5b7c5f16fd85ce245ef0f07e8b2f76f6a6
Author: Trevor Bača <trevorbaca@gmail.com>
Date:   Sun Apr 5 18:26:21 2015 -0400

    Improved tuplet number formatting corner case.
    
    OLD:
    
        This worked:
    
        >>> tuplet = Tuplet((2, 3), "c'8 c' c'")
        >>> override(tuplet).tuplet_number.text = Markup('foo')
    
        But this did not work:
    
        >>> tuplet = Tuplet((3, 5), "c'8 c' c' c' c'")
        >>> override(tuplet).tuplet_number.text = Markup('foo')
    
    NEW: Both examples now work.
    
    Explanation: Abjad treats tuplets-that-fit-into-non-power-of-two-durations in a
    way such that fraction text (like 5:3) always appears. This is good because "5"
    is ambiguous and probabaly means 5:4 ... which makes printing "5" especially
    bad if the tuplet ratio is actually 5:3. But this special-casing of such
    tuplets was preventing the ability to override tuplet number text explicitly.
    This commit extends the special-casing code and makes it possible to override
    tuplet number text explicitly for the first time.
    
    Doesn't need to be included in upcoming release notes.

commit 07eb130f85b32d29338cd32e3a2db82f787844dc
Author: Josiah Wolf Oberholtzer <josiah.oberholtzer@gmail.com>
Date:   Sun Apr 5 16:41:09 2015 -0700

    Activated "period" keyword in Retrogression and Rotation.
    
    Use "period" to rotate or retrograde periodic subsegments of a pitch-object
    segment.
    
    Periodic retrogression:
    
        >>> operator_ = pitchtools.Retrogression(period=3)
        >>> pitches = pitchtools.PitchSegment("c' d' e' f' g' a' b' c''")
        >>> operator_(pitches)
        PitchSegment(["e'", "d'", "c'", "a'", "g'", "f'", "c''", "b'"])
    
    Periodic rotation without transposition:
    
        >>> operator_ = pitchtools.Rotation(
        ...     index=1,
        ...     period=3,
        ...     transpose=False,
        ...     )
        >>> pitches = pitchtools.PitchSegment("c' d' e' f' g' a' b' c''")
        >>> operator_(pitches)
        PitchSegment(["e'", "c'", "d'", "a'", "f'", "g'", "c''", "b'"])
    
    Periodic rotation with transposition:
    
        >>> operator_ = pitchtools.Rotation(
        ...     index=1,
        ...     period=3,
        ...     )
        >>> pitches = pitchtools.PitchSegment("c' d' e' f' g' a' b' c''")
        >>> operator_(pitches)
        PitchSegment(["c'", 'af', 'bf', "f'", "df'", "ef'", "b'", "as'"])

commit 5ed612e0dc3e5025f562109807af4eb239cb5771
Author: Josiah Wolf Oberholtzer <josiah.oberholtzer@gmail.com>
Date:   Sun Apr 5 17:30:36 2015 -0700

    Added Duplication to sequencetools.
    
    This class models the process of duplicating items in a sequence periodically.
    
    Duplicates once without period:
    
        >>> operator_ = sequencetools.Duplication(count=1)
        >>> numbers = [1, 2, 3, 4]
        >>> operator_(numbers)
        [1, 2, 3, 4, 1, 2, 3, 4]
    
    Duplicates twice without period:
    
        >>> operator_ = sequencetools.Duplication(count=2)
        >>> pitch_classes = pitchtools.PitchClassSegment([0, 1, 4, 7])
        >>> operator_(pitch_classes)
        PitchClassSegment([0, 1, 4, 7, 0, 1, 4, 7, 0, 1, 4, 7])
    
    Duplicates once periodically:
    
        >>> operator_ = sequencetools.Duplication(count=1, period=3)
        >>> pitches = pitchtools.PitchSegment("c' d' e' f' g' a' b' c''")
        >>> for pitch in operator_(pitches):
        ...     pitch
        ...
        NamedPitch("c'")
        NamedPitch("d'")
        NamedPitch("e'")
        NamedPitch("c'")
        NamedPitch("d'")
        NamedPitch("e'")
        NamedPitch("f'")
        NamedPitch("g'")
        NamedPitch("a'")
        NamedPitch("f'")
        NamedPitch("g'")
        NamedPitch("a'")
        NamedPitch("b'")
        NamedPitch("c''")
        NamedPitch("b'")
        NamedPitch("c''")

        >>> tuplet = Tuplet((5, 7), "c'16 c' c' c' c' c' c'")

commit d74aad55f6436f2687c971f81aea4abee0e452cf
Author: Trevor Bača <trevorbaca@gmail.com>

    Restructured AccelerandoRhythmMaker output.
    
    OLD: AccelerandoRhythmMaker ouptut a list of selections that each comprised
    one or more notes.

commit d7beaa60b51c92208b8f4ff18968a6e7b1690613
Author: Trevor Bača <trevorbaca@gmail.com>
Date:   Sun Apr 5 23:37:32 2015 -0400

    Added Tuplet.force_times_command property. NEW.
    
    Trivial tuplets normally print with no LilyPond \times command:
    
        >>> trivial_tuplet = Tuplet((1, 1), "c'4 d' e'")
        >>> trivial_tuplet.force_times_command
        False
    
        >>> f(trivial_tuplet)
        {
            c'4
            d'4
            e'4
        }
    
    Set the new Tuplet.force_times_command property to true to force even trivial
    tuplets to format the LilyPond \times command:
    
        >>> trivial_tuplet = Tuplet((1, 1), "c'4 d' e'")
        >>> trivial_tuplet.force_times_command = True
    
        >>> f(trivial_tuplet)
        \times 1/1 {
            c'4
            d'4
            e'4
        }
    
    This makes it possible to override tuplet number text because LilyPond now
    renders a tuplet bracket:
    
        >>> trivial_tuplet = Tuplet((1, 1), "c'4 d' e'")
        >>> trivial_tuplet.force_times_command = True
        >>> duration = inspect_(trivial_tuplet).get_duration()
        >>> markup = duration.to_score_markup()
        >>> markup = markup.scale((0.75, 0.75))
        >>> override(trivial_tuplet).tuplet_number.text = markup
        >>> staff = Staff([trivial_tuplet])
    
    NEW: should be included (with notated example from above) in the 2.16 release
    notes.

Author: Trevor Bača <trevorbaca@gmail.com>
Date:   Mon Apr 6 10:39:59 2015 -0400

    Alphabetized BooleanPattern initializer keyword. NOTE.
    
    OLD:
    
        BooleanPattern.__init__(
            indices=None,
            period=None,
            start=None,
            stop=None,
            invert=None,
            )
    
    NEW:
    
        BooleanPattern.__init__(
            indices=None,
            invert=None,
            period=None,
            start=None,
            stop=None,
            )
    
    Note that this may break client code that relied on the position of keywords.
    
    Use explicit keyword names to avoid.

        >>> maker = rhythmmakertools.NoteRhythmMaker()

        ...     indices=[0, 1, 7],

        1 NoteRhythmMaker()
        2
        3
        4
        5
        6
        7 NoteRhythmMaker()
        8 NoteRhythmMaker()
        9 NoteRhythmMaker()

commit 43f7fe42ed79a11e4baf27eeb2dd0b59ae05bb12
Author: Trevor Bača <trevorbaca@gmail.com>
Date:   Mon Apr 6 14:53:43 2015 -0400

    Added BooleanPatternInventory.get_matching_payload() method.
    
    Example: Here's a way to specify notes for all indices except for the last
    three indices, to which even divisions are assinged:
    
        >>> inventory = rhythmmakertools.BooleanPatternInventory([
        ...     rhythmmakertools.BooleanPattern(
        ...         indices=[0],
        ...         payload=rhythmmakertools.NoteRhythmMaker(),
        ...         period=1,
        ...         ),
        ...     rhythmmakertools.BooleanPattern(
        ...         indices=[-3, -2, -1],
        ...         payload=rhythmmakertools.EvenDivisionRhythmMaker(),
        ...         ),
        ...     ])
    
        >>> for i in range(10):
        ...     match = inventory.get_matching_payload(i, 10)
        ...     print(i, match)
        ...
        0 NoteRhythmMaker()
        1 NoteRhythmMaker()
        2 NoteRhythmMaker()
        3 NoteRhythmMaker()
        4 NoteRhythmMaker()
        5 NoteRhythmMaker()
        6 NoteRhythmMaker()
        7 EvenDivisionRhythmMaker(denominators=(8,))
        8 EvenDivisionRhythmMaker(denominators=(8,))
        9 EvenDivisionRhythmMaker(denominators=(8,))

commit 88e452ee81287ea68ca00eb14365e1ea241d716d

commit 462e5e70a1226f22db61b7d8ff24a3ca52b5eac2
Author: Josiah Wolf Oberholtzer <josiah.oberholtzer@gmail.com>
Date:   Mon Apr 6 15:42:02 2015 -0700

    Integrated NullMask into RhythmMaker.
    
    Use NullMask in a rhythm-maker's output masks inventory to prevent the
    rhythm-maker from operating on certain divisions.
    
    Without NullMask:
    
        >>> divisions = [(4, 8), (3, 8), (4, 8), (3, 8), (2, 8)]
        >>> rest_mask = rhythmmakertools.SilenceMask(
        ...     indices=[0],
        ...     period=2,
        ...     )
        >>> maker = rhythmmakertools.NoteRhythmMaker(
        ...     output_masks=[rest_mask],
        ...     )
        >>> music = maker(divisions)
        >>> staff = maker._get_rhythmic_staff(lilypond_file)
        >>> f(staff)
        \new RhythmicStaff {
            {
                \time 4/8
                r2
            }
            {
                \time 3/8
                c'4.
            }
            {
                \time 4/8
                r2
            }
            {
                \time 3/8
                c'4.
            }
            {
                \time 2/8
                r4
            }
        }
    
    With NullMask:
    
        >>> null_mask = rhythmmakertools.NullMask(
        ...     indices=[0, -1],
        ...     )
        >>> maker = rhythmmakertools.NoteRhythmMaker(
        ...     output_masks=[rest_mask, null_mask],
        ...     )
        >>> music = maker(divisions)
        >>> staff = maker._get_rhythmic_staff(lilypond_file)
        >>> f(staff)
        \new RhythmicStaff {
            {
                \time 4/8
                c'2
            }
            {
                \time 3/8
                c'4.
            }
            {
                \time 4/8
                r2
            }
            {
                \time 3/8
                c'4.
            }
            {
                \time 2/8
                c'4
            }
        }

commit 5ca3a81f2e695b0449bcce136d831b46f67c989e
Author: Trevor Bača <trevorbaca@gmail.com>
Date:   Mon Apr 6 21:42:26 2015 -0400

    Added remember_state=False keyword to all rhythm-maker __call__() methods. NEW.
    
    The keyword is fully active in EvenDivisionRhythmMaker.
    
    The keyword has not yet integrated into the other rhythm-makers.
    
    Examples: rebuild the docs and see the EvenDivisionRhythmMaker.__call__
    docstring before contrastive examples.
    
    Explanation: Takes advantage of the magic state-preservation features of Python
    generators. A new static helper method is implemented on RhythmMaker:
    
        @staticmethod
        def _make_cyclic_tuple_generator(iterable):
            cyclic_tuple = datastructuretools.CyclicTuple(iterable)
            i = 0
            while True:
                yield cyclic_tuple[i]
                i += 1
    
    The method wraps a cyclic tuple in a generator. The method is called *at the
    end of initialization*. The generator is stored on the object created at the
    end of initialization. This adds only a single extra line (per iterable) to the
    rhythm-maker initializer. Here're the relevant lines in
    EvenDivisionRhythmMaker:
    
            self._denominators_generator = self._make_cyclic_tuple_generator(
                denominators)
            self._extra_counts_per_division_generator = \
                self._make_cyclic_tuple_generator(extra_counts_per_division)
    
    Call-time behavior then checks the remember_state flag. If remember_state is
    false then music-making proceeds as before. If remember_state is true then
    values are obtained for the generators cached during initialization. This
    amounts to two extra lines in EvenDivisionRhythmMaker:
    
                if remember_state:
                    denominator = self._denominators_generator.next()
                    extra_count = self._extra_counts_per_division_generator.next()
                else:
                    denominator = denominators[i]
                    extra_count = extra_counts_per_division[i]
    
    This technique will absolutely work for all iterables in all rhythm-makers.
    
    The question is deciding whether we want the functionality implemented or not.

commit f0d51e122d84669d9c1bdcc76d12fc63c4859f60
Author: Trevor Bača <trevorbaca@gmail.com>
Date:   Tue Apr 7 11:47:53 2015 -0400

    Adjusted TypedOrderedDict item coercion.
    
    OLD: TypedOrderedDict did not coerce items during initialization.
    
    NEW: TypedOrderedDict does coerce items during initialization.

commit 68428ea4e6c2f93ee4c31958b0d6adfbde0dc0e9
Author: Trevor Bača <trevorbaca@gmail.com>
Date:   Tue Apr 7 11:48:46 2015 -0400

    Added new PartitionTable class to rhythmmakertools.
    
    The class inherits from TypedOrderedDict.
    
    The class provides a way for composers to specify arbitrary ratios used for
    dividing temporal objects.
    
    For example, The integer 7 can be entered in the table as 7 = 4 + 3 or
    as 7 = 1 + 6. (This expresses an integer partition as a ratio.)
    
    Some of the rhythm-makers will integrate PartitionTable to customize tuplet
    creation and other parts of rhythmic output.

    Set "spell_metrically" to true to spell unassignable talea values metrically:
    
        >>> leaves = scoretools.make_leaves_from_talea(
        ...     [3, -3, 5, -5], 16,
        ...     spell_metrically='unassignable',
        ...     )
        >>> staff = Staff(leaves)
        >>> staff.context_name = 'RhythmicStaff'
        >>> time_signature = TimeSignature((4, 4))
        >>> attach(time_signature, staff)
        >>> print(format(staff))
        \new RhythmicStaff {
            \time 4/4
            c'8.
            r8.
            c'8. ~
            c'8
            r8.
            r8
        }

commit 1de0a797b196514d8ae9b0016d5a1fad6007219e
Author: Josiah Wolf Oberholtzer <josiah.oberholtzer@gmail.com>
Date:   Thu Apr 9 12:21:00 2015 -0700

    Extended Selector.by_duration() with "preprolated=None" keyword.
    
    Set "preprolated" to true to select components based on their preprolated
    durations. For example, this is useful for selecting note and chords -- and any
    logical ties comprising them -- by their written durations, regardless of any
    tuplets in their parentage:
    
    ::
    
        >>> staff = Staff(r"""
        ... \times 3/4 { c'16 d'16 ~ d'16 e'16 ~ }
        ... { e'16 f'16 ~ f'16 g'16 ~ }
        ... \times 5/4 { g'16 a'16 ~ a'16 b'16 }
        ... """)
    
    ::
    
        >>> selector = selectortools.Selector()
        >>> selector = selector.by_logical_tie()
        >>> selector = selector.by_duration(
        ...     '==',
        ...     (1, 8),
        ...     preprolated=True,
        ...     )
    
    ::
    
        >>> selections = selector(staff)
        >>> for logical_tie in selections:
        ...     attach(Articulation('accent'), logical_tie[0])
        ...     print(logical_tie)
        ...
        LogicalTie(Note("d'16"), Note("d'16"))
        LogicalTie(Note("e'16"), Note("e'16"))
        LogicalTie(Note("f'16"), Note("f'16"))
        LogicalTie(Note("g'16"), Note("g'16"))
        LogicalTie(Note("a'16"), Note("a'16"))

commit 49c3a1410c5358e8a4458bf17a8f615013ff5b52
Author: Trevor Bača <trevorbaca@gmail.com>
Date:   Thu Apr 9 22:25:39 2015 -0400

    Activated partition-table duration spelling in NoteRhythmMaker. NEW.
    
    Allows for arbitrary spell of any division based on numerator.
    
    Usage:
    
        1. build partition table
        2. assign partition table to duration spelling specifier
    
    Example:
    
        >>> partition_table = rhythmmakertools.PartitionTable([
        ...     (5, [3, 2]),
        ...     (9, [3, 3, 3]),
        ...     ])
        >>> maker = rhythmmakertools.NoteRhythmMaker(
        ...     duration_spelling_specifier=rhythmmakertools.DurationSpellingSpecifier(
        ...         spell_metrically=partition_table,
        ...         ),
        ...     )
    
    The example above ensure that all durations of the form 5/x (and also 10/x and
    20/x etc.) are spelled in the ratio of 3/x + 2/x.
    
    See the NoteRhythmMaker API entry for notated examples.

commit 46d64b79275dbbaa4602b24a81028963fa85be12
Author: Josiah Wolf Oberholtzer <josiah.oberholtzer@gmail.com>
Date:   Fri Apr 10 17:25:37 2015 -0700

    Extended new() and wrote new() tests.
    
    Given a class like so:
    
        class Aggregate(abctools.AbjadValueObject):
    
            __slots__ = ('_pitch_segment', '_ratio')
    
            def __init__(self, pitch_segment=None, ratio=None):
                if pitch_segment is not None:
                    pitch_segment = pitchtools.PitchSegment(pitch_segment)
                self._pitch_segment = pitch_segment
                if ratio is not None:
                    ratio = mathtools.Ratio(ratio)
                self._ratio = ratio
    
            @property
            def pitch_segment(self):
                return self._pitch_segment
    
            @property
            def ratio(self):
                return self._ratio
    
    ... you can now use new() to not only replace, but also call generating methods
    on subkeys as well:
    
        >>> old_aggregate = Aggregate(
        ...    pitch_segment=pitchtools.PitchSegment('c d e f'),
        ...    ratio=mathtools.Ratio([1, 2, 3])
        ...    )
        >>> new_aggregate = new(
        ...     old_aggregate
        ...     ratio=[4, 5],
        ...     pitch_segment__rotate=2,
        ...     )
        >>> print(format(new_aggregate))
        Aggregate(
            pitch_segment=pitchtools.PitchSegment(
                (
                    pitchtools.NamedPitch('e'),
                    pitchtools.NamedPitch('f'),
                    pitchtools.NamedPitch('c'),
                    pitchtools.NamedPitch('d'),
                    ),
                item_class=pitchtools.NamedPitch,
                ),
            ratio=mathtools.Ratio((4, 5)),
            )

commit 8b8f93415938538f5490d3c6c163b3a75e50fc94
Author: Trevor Bača <trevorbaca@gmail.com>
Date:   Sat Apr 11 15:42:02 2015 -0400

    Activated TupletSpellingSpecifier.flatten_trivial_tuplets in rhythm-makers.
    
    New functionality.
    
    See TupletRhythmMaker.tuplet_spelling_specifier docstring for examples.
    
    NOTE: the motivation here is the fact that untupletted notes can be
    meter-rewritten in ways that tupletted notes can not. So there's a real-world
    benefit to setting flatten_trivial_tuplets=True if you then subsequently
    rewrite the meters of the rhythms produced.

commit 814913ccd7d0802e7e48f9e9367c4d5316370c92
Author: Josiah Wolf Oberholtzer <josiah.oberholtzer@gmail.com>
Date:   Mon Apr 13 12:37:03 2015 -0700

    Added StaffLinesSpanner.forbid_restarting property.
    
    Set to true to prevent the spanner from re-stopping and re-starting the staff
    on its last leaf. This is useful to prevent LilyPond from exhibiting unusual
    typesetting behavior when a stopping and starting the staff on the final leaf
    of a context.

    Added Selector.run_selectors() static method. NEW.
    
    Use this method to run multiple selectors against a single selection. The
    method conserves the amount of re-selection done by each selector by
    maintaining interim selections according to identical sequences of selector
    callbacks.

commit c886b0fa2b1bc2c117741c8ace2a13530661e105
Author: Trevor Bača <trevorbaca@gmail.com>
Date:   Wed Apr 15 15:31:24 2015 -0400

    Added Scheme.verbatim property. NEW.
    
    Defaults to false.
    
    Set to true to bypass Scheme formatting entirely. This leaves whitespace and
    quotes in tact. And is apparently the only way to concoct certain expressions
    that contain things like nested markup with quoted string arguments.
    
    Example.
    
        >>> string = '(lambda (grob) (grob-interpret-markup grob'
        >>> string += r' #{ \markup \musicglyph #"noteheads.s0harmonic" #}))'
        >>> scheme = schemetools.Scheme(string, verbatim=True)
        Scheme('(lambda (grob) (grob-interpret-markup grob #{ \\markup \\musicglyph #"noteheads.s0harmonic" #}))')
        >>> print(format(scheme))
        #(lambda (grob) (grob-interpret-markup grob #{ \markup \musicglyph #"noteheads.s0harmonic" #}))
    
    NEW. Should be included in the 2.16 release notes.

commit 1b7afb7b10c2817e7ba605d0254533ebd535fccf
Author: Trevor Bača <trevorbaca@gmail.com>
Date:   Wed Apr 15 15:33:11 2015 -0400

    Added TrillSpanner.is_harmonic property. NEW.
    
    Defaults to false.
    
    Set to true to format the trill pitch note head as a white diamond.
    
    Example:
    
        >>> staff = Staff("c'8 d'8 e'8 f'8")
        >>> trill = spannertools.TrillSpanner(
                is_harmonic=True,
                pitch=NamedPitch("d'"),
                )
        >>> attach(trill, staff[:])
    
        >>> f(staff)
        \new Staff {
            \once \override TrillPitchHead #'stencil = #(lambda (grob) (grob-interpret-markup grob #{ \markup \musicglyph #"noteheads.s0harmonic" #}))
            \pitchedTrill
            c'8 \startTrillSpan d'
            d'8
            e'8
            f'8 \stopTrillSpan
        }
    
    NEW. Should be included in the 2.16 release notes.

commit 44ceecee2730be74c9c4a17ce43d9bd1bcecb45c
Author: Josiah Wolf Oberholtzer <josiah.oberholtzer@gmail.com>
Date:   Wed Apr 22 22:05:57 2015 -0700

    Extended InspectionAgent.get_spanner() with "in_parentage" keyword.
    
    Set "in_parentage" to true to check for spanners not only on the inspected
    component, but also any components in its parentage. This affords composers
    the means to easily test if a component is covered by a spanner.
    
    Also extended .get_spanners() and .has_spanner() with "in_parentage".
